\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{t}{t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a152339e6ee653f666802b0f8708a0ec3}{t}} =  t\+\_\+0 \textbackslash{}f\$ and \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a152339e6ee653f666802b0f8708a0ec3}{t}}=t\+\_\+0 + \textbackslash{}Delta \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a152339e6ee653f666802b0f8708a0ec3}{t}} \textbackslash{}f\$. At \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a152339e6ee653f666802b0f8708a0ec3}{t}}=t\+\_\+0 + 2 \textbackslash{}Delta \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a152339e6ee653f666802b0f8708a0ec3}{t}} \textbackslash{}f\$, \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} automatic \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_abf750b8569ba0accd1c8ea606f8bd508}{mesh}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_af6873b0727abfbb225ff73d92ca1536e}{adaptation}} splits one \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} fluid elements, creating \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} five new \textbackslash{}c Nodes, shown in red (for simplicity we only show \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} fluid elements\textquotesingle{} vertex nodes). Their position \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad8a01f7025d090c6b28ca935f5f71bc6}{is}} determined by \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} father element\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_abe1a872647b7cfc1c732b57adef7d1b9}{s}} \textbackslash{}c Macro\+Element mapping, using \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} current position \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} \textbackslash{}c Mesh\+As\+Geom\+Object, obtained from \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} interpolation between \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} nodal \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a33217aaaae3d8be0cd7f2377e92255da}{positions}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} its \textbackslash{}c Solid\+Nodes (shown as green circles). @I w 0.\+75\textbackslash{}textwidth history\+\_\+values \char`\"{}Sketch illustrating \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} assignment \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} positional history \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae5713822b0ed99d2fb3a40c0f0ceda24}{values}} for newly-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad4e59dc52f697b1186d8a14191c9c8c9}{created}} nodes in F\+SI problems. The positional history \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae5713822b0ed99d2fb3a40c0f0ceda24}{values}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} newly-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad4e59dc52f697b1186d8a14191c9c8c9}{created}} Nodes (shown in red) are given by \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a33217aaaae3d8be0cd7f2377e92255da}{positions}} they would have had if they had already existed at previous timesteps. \char`\"{} So far, so good! A subtle problem arises when we try to assign \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} positional history \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae5713822b0ed99d2fb3a40c0f0ceda24}{values}} for \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} newly-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad4e59dc52f697b1186d8a14191c9c8c9}{created}} \textbackslash{}c Nodes. The evaluation \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} \textbackslash{}c Macro\+Element mapping at \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} previous timesteps (required to determine \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a33217aaaae3d8be0cd7f2377e92255da}{positions}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} newly-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad4e59dc52f697b1186d8a14191c9c8c9}{created}} \textbackslash{}c Nodes would have had, if they had already existed at previous timesteps) requires access to \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} previous wall shapes. In $<$A H\+R\+EF=\char`\"{}../../../navier\+\_\+stokes/collapsible\+\_\+channel/html/index.\+html\char`\"{}$>$ the non-\/F\+SI problem discussed earlier$<$/A$>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} wall shape was given analytically and could therefore be evaluated at arbitrary times. In \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} F\+SI problem considered here, \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} previous wall shape \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad8a01f7025d090c6b28ca935f5f71bc6}{is}} not available as \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} previous \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a33217aaaae3d8be0cd7f2377e92255da}{positions}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} \textbackslash{}c Solid\+Nodes are not required (and are therefore not stored) for \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} solution \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_a63db2bdb4f52051f8eedaa4d840052a0}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} (steady!) wall equations. $<$HR$>$ \textbackslash{}subsection soln The solution\+: The Steady$<$N\+S\+T\+E\+PS$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_af2d66f9241d0dbe70895113b7f62a71b}{timestepper}} The solution to \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ae3472ac0ca382c5891ce00bc933b3d82}{the}} problem \mbox{\hyperlink{fsi__collapsible__channel__adapt_8txt_ad8a01f7025d090c6b28ca935f5f71bc6}{is}}
